2.2.3

3.2.2
\[+\frac{(x_4)(x_9)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_4)(x_9)(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)}{(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_4)(x_0)(x_9)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_4)(x_9)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)}{(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_4)(x_9)(x_2)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)}{(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_4)(x_9)(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)(1-x_9)}{(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_4)(x_0)(x_9)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)(1-x_9)}{(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_4)(x_9)(x_2)(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)(1-x_2)}{(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_4)(x_0)(x_9)(x_2)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)(1-x_2)}{(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1- 3.2.3

3.2.4
\[+\frac{(x_8)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_9)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_10)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_0)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_8)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_8)(x_9)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)(1-x_9)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_8)(x_10)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)(1-x_9)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_8)(x_0)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)(1-x_9)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_8)(x_9)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}( 3.2.5
\[+\frac{(x_8)(x_0)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_1)(x_8)(x_0)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_0)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_0)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{\frac{1}{2}(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_1)(x_8)(x_0)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(x_0)(1-x_1)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_1)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(x_0)(1-x_1)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x \[+\frac{(x_8)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_9)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_10)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_8)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_8)(x_9)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)(1-x_9)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_8)(x_10)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)(1-x_9)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_8)(x_9)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{4(A)^{2}(x_8)(x_10)(x_9)(1-x_8)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{\frac{3}{2}(A)^{2}(x_8)(x^{2}+x_10)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{\frac{1}{2}(A)^{2}(x_8)(x^{2}+x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[-\frac{(A)^{2}(x_8)(x_9)(1-x_8)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{re \[+\frac{(x_8)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_1)(x_8)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{\frac{1}{2}(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_1)(x_8)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(1-x_1)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(x_10)(1-x_1)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_8)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{4(A)^{2}(x_8)(x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)(1-x_10)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{\frac{3}{2}(A)^{2}(x_8)(x^{2}+x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[-\frac{(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(1-x_1)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red} \[+\frac{(x_1)(x_5)(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)(x_6)(x_5)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)(1-x_6)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)(x_4)(x_5)(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)(1-x_4)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_1)(x_5)(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_6)(x_5)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_4)(x_5)(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_1)(x^{2}+x_6)(x_5)(1-x_1)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_6)(x_4)(x_5)(1-x_1)(1-x_6)(1-x_4)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_1)(x^{2}+x_4)(x_5)(1-x_1)(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_6)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]

\[+\frac{(x_9)(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)}{(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_12)(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_0)(x_9)(1-x_9)(1-x_0)}{(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_12)(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_9)(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_12)(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{\frac{1}{2}(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_0)(x_9)(1-x_9)}{(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_12)(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_0)(x_9)(1-x_0)}{(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_12)(1-x_3)}\]\[-\frac{\frac{1}{2}(A)^{2}(x_0)(x_9)(1-x_0)(1-x_9)}{(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_12)(1-x_3)}\]

\[+\frac{(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_9)(x_8)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)(1-x_8)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_9)(x_4)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)(1-x_4)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_8)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_9)(x^{2}+x_8)(1-x_9)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_8)(x_4)(1-x_9)(1-x_8)(1-x_4)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_4)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_9)(x^{2}+x_4)(1-x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_5)}\]

8.2.1
\[+\frac{(x_2)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_9)(x_2)(x_0)(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_2)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_2)(x_4)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_2)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_9)(x_2)(x_0)(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_2)(x_0)(1-x_9)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_2)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{3(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_2)(x_4)(x_0)(1-x_9)(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{3(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_2)(x_0)(1-x_9)(1-x_2)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_2) 8.2.2
\[+\frac{(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_9)(x_0)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_4)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_9)(x_0)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{3(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_8)(x_0)(1-x_9)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{3(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_4)(x_0)(1-x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{3(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_0)(1-x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\tex \[+\frac{(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(x_8)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(x_4)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(x^{2}+x_8)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{4(A)^{2}(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(x_8)(x_4)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)(1-x_4)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{4(A)^{2}(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(x_8)(1-x_8)(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(x^{2}+x_4)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{4(A)^{2}(x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(x_4)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{4}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_4)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{\frac{3}{2}(A)^{2}(x_1)(x^{2}+x_1)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_4)^ \[+\frac{(x_1)(x_10)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)(x_8)(x_10)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)(x_10)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_1)(x_10)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)(x^{2}+x_8)(x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{4(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{4(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{\frac{3}{2}(A)^{2}(x_1)(x^{2}+x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\tex 8.2.5
\[+\frac{(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_9)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_9)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_8)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_9)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{3(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_8)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_9)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{3(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_9)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_0)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}}\]\[-\frac{3(A)^{2}(x_9)(x_10)(x_0)(1-x_9)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_0)}{(1-x_9)^ \[+\frac{(x_1)(x_10)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)(x_8)(x_10)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{2(A)(x_1)(x_10)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{(A)(x_1)(x_10)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[-\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)(x^{2}+x_8)(x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[-\frac{4(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)(1-x_10)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[-\frac{\frac{3}{2}(A)^{2}(x_1)(x^{2}+x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(x_10)(1-x_8)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[+\frac{(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_10)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)(1-x_1)}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[-\frac{(A)^{2}(x^{2}+x_1)(x_10)(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_3)}\]\[-\frac{2(A)^{2}(x_1)(x_8)(x_10)(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}(1-x_8)(1-x_10)^{\textcolor{red}{2}}}{(1-x_1)^{\textcolor{red}{3}}(1-x_8)^{\textcolor{red
